   ],
   "source": [
    "cap = cv2.VideoCapture(0)  # Use 0 for the default camera\n",
    "\n",
    "while cap.isOpened():\n",
    "    ret, frame = cap.read()\n",
    "    if not ret:\n",
    "        break\n",
    "\n",
    "    # Convert the BGR image to RGB\n",
    "    rgb_frame = cv2.cvtColor(frame, cv2.COLOR_BGR2RGB)\n",
    "    \n",
    "    # Process the image with MediaPipe Pose\n",
    "    results = pose.process(rgb_frame)\n",
    "\n",
    "    # Draw pose landmarks\n",
    "    if results.pose_landmarks:\n",
    "        mp.solutions.drawing_utils.draw_landmarks(frame, results.pose_landmarks, mp_pose.POSE_CONNECTIONS)\n",
    "    \n",
    "    # Preprocess the frame for classification\n",
    "    resized_frame = cv2.resize(frame, (224, 224))\n",
    "    img_array = image.img_to_array(resized_frame)\n",
    "    img_array = np.expand_dims(img_array, axis=0)\n",
    "    img_array /= 255.0  # Rescale like the training data\n",
    "\n",
    "    # Make a prediction\n",
    "    prediction = model.predict(img_array)\n",
    "    predicted_class_idx = np.argmax(prediction)\n",
    "    predicted_class_name = class_labels[predicted_class_idx]\n",
    "\n",
    "    # Display the result\n",
    "    cv2.putText(frame, f\"Pose: {predicted_class_name}\", (10, 30), cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 1, (0, 255, 0), 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "    # Show the frame\n",
    "    cv2.imshow('Yoga Pose Classification', frame)\n",
    "\n",
    "    # Exit on 'q' key\n",
    "    if cv2.waitKey(1) & 0xFF == ord('q'):\n",
    "        break\n",
    "\n",
    "# Release resources\n",
    "cap.release()\n",
    "cv2.destroyAllWindows()"
   ]
  },
